- diagnosis: The task is to assess the likely AIE mechanism for a large hydrocarbon polyaryl molecule. From the input structure and shared prepared context, the current top1 working hypothesis is neutral aromatic, and the current top2 runner-up is ICT. A still-credible third candidate, TICT, also remains in the portfolio because the molecule has several phenyl rotors and five torsion candidates. Top1 is still uncertain because the current evidence is mostly structural: the molecule is heteroatom-free and strongly aromatic, which disfavors ESIPT and weakens classical donor-acceptor ICT logic, but this alone does not decide whether the emissive/nonemissive behavior is best viewed as a neutral aromatic restricted-motion case or whether twisting-driven excited-state relaxation remains important. Shared prepared structure context is available and ready, which supports one bounded microscopic baseline calculation on the selected conformer. Macro can screen one deterministic structural evidence family from the registry, but cannot make a global mechanism decision. Microscopic can perform exactly one low-cost baseline S0/S1 action and can provide only initial excited-state clues, not full conformer or torsion sensitivity. Both Macro and Microscopic should be used in round 1 because together they provide complementary indirect evidence: macro topology for rotor-rich neutral-aromatic versus twisting plausibility, and baseline S0/S1 electronic behavior for whether unexpected CT-like character appears. The case remains in portfolio screening rather than pairwise contraction because at least one non-top2 credible alternative, TICT, has not yet been screened or dropped by evidence.

- status: success

- task_received: Current reasoning phase: portfolio_screening. Agent framing mode: portfolio_neutral. Reuse the shared prepared structure context when available, summarize low-cost structural indicators only, and stay within current macro capability. Hypothesis uncertainty to keep in mind: Neutral aromatic leads because the molecule is an all-carbon aromatic framework with no ESIPT motif and no obvious donor-acceptor segmentation, but the presence of multiple phenyl rotors means a twisting-based excited-state pathway still needs explicit screening, and baseline electronic evidence is needed before ICT can be confidently downweighted further.

- task_completion_status: completed

- task_completion: Task completed successfully within current macro capability.

- task_understanding: The task is to assess macro-level structural evidence relevant to the current working hypothesis 'neutral aromatic' by reusing the shared prepared structure context and summarizing low-cost structural indicators within the current macro capability limits.

- reasoning_summary: The molecule is an all-carbon aromatic framework with no ESIPT motif or obvious donor-acceptor segmentation, supporting the neutral aromatic hypothesis as a provisional lead. However, multiple phenyl rotors suggest potential twisting-based excited-state pathways that require explicit screening. Baseline electronic evidence is needed before confidently downweighting ICT. Therefore, structural evidence focusing on aromatic core dominance, ring-system rigidity, and neutral-aromatic structural cues is most relevant at this stage.
Capability limit note: Only deterministic low-cost single-molecule macro analysis is available. Aggregate-state modeling, packing simulation, and global mechanism adjudication are unsupported.

- execution_plan: Use deterministic_macro_structure_scan to execute the bounded registry-backed macro capability `screen_neutral_aromatic_structure` with focus areas: aromatic core, ring system rigidity, neutral aromatic structural cues. Planned local steps: [shared_context_load] Load the shared prepared structure context and reuse its descriptors. [focus_selection] Translate the Planner instruction into one bounded registry-backed macro capability. [topology_analysis] Collect deterministic structural evidence for `screen_neutral_aromatic_structure` from the available structure source. [geometry_proxy_analysis] Summarize only bounded local structural or geometry-proxy outputs and record any missing deliverables.

- result_summary: Bounded neutral-aromatic structural screening summarized aromatic-core dominance, ring-system organization, and rigid-core geometry proxies from the available structural context. The macro scan recorded aromatic_atom_count=48, hetero_atom_count=0, branch_point_count=14, rotatable_bond_count=5, planarity_proxy=0.821691, compactness_proxy=0.92526, and conformer_dispersion_proxy=1.0.
Key proxies: aromatic_atom_count=48, hetero_atom_count=0, branch_point_count=14, conjugation_proxy=12.822, flexibility_proxy=13.0, rotatable_bond_count=5, aromatic_ring_count=8, ring_system_count=5, donor_acceptor_partition_proxy=0.0, planarity_proxy=0.821691, compactness_proxy=0.92526, conformer_dispersion_proxy=1.0.
